# writeContract · Viem

[Skip to content](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#vocs-content)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

Search...

⌘

K

writeContract
=============

Executes a write function on a contract.

A "write" function on a Solidity contract modifies the state of the blockchain. These types of functions require gas to be executed, and hence a [Transaction](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms)
 is needed to be broadcast in order to change the state.

Internally, `writeContract` uses a [Wallet Client](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet)
 to call the [`sendTransaction` action](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction)
 with [ABI-encoded `data`](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/encodeFunctionData)
.

Usage[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#usage)

-----------------------------------------------------------

Below is a very basic example of how to execute a write function on a contract (with no arguments).

While you can use `writeContract` [by itself](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#standalone)
, it is highly recommended to pair it with `[simulateContract](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/simulateContract) ` to validate that the contract write will execute without errors.

example.tsabi.tsconfig.ts

    import { account, publicClient, walletClient } from './config'
    import { wagmiAbi } from './abi'
     
    const { request } = await publicClient.simulateContract({
      account,
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
    })
    await walletClient.writeContract(request)

### Passing Arguments[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#passing-arguments)

If your function requires argument(s), you can pass them through with the `args` attribute.

TypeScript types for `args` will be inferred from the function name & ABI, to guard you from inserting the wrong values.

For example, the `mint` function name below requires a **tokenId** argument, and it is typed as `[number]`.

example.tsabi.tsconfig.ts

    import { account, walletClient } from './client'
    import { wagmiAbi } from './abi'
     
    const { request } = await publicClient.simulateContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      account
    })
    await walletClient.writeContract(request)

### Standalone[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#standalone)

If you don't need to perform validation on the contract write, you can also use it by itself:

example.tsabi.tsconfig.ts

    import { account, walletClient } from './config'
    import { wagmiAbi } from './abi'
     
    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      account,
    })

Return Value[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#return-value)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[Hash](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#hash) `

A [Transaction Hash](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#hash)
.

Unlike `[readContract](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/readContract) `, `writeContract` only returns a [Transaction Hash](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#hash)
. If you would like to retrieve the return data of a write function, you can use the [`simulateContract` action](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/simulateContract)
 – this action does not execute a transaction, and does not require gas (it is very similar to `readContract`).

Parameters[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

### address[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#address)

*   **Type:** `[Address](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#address) `

The contract address.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2', 
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420]
    })

### abi[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#abi)

*   **Type:** `[Abi](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#abi) `

The contract's ABI.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi, 
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420]
    })

### functionName[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#functionname)

*   **Type:** `string`

A function to extract from the ABI.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint', 
      args: [69420]
    })

### account[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#account)

*   **Type:** `Account | Address | null`

The Account to write to the contract from.

Accepts a [JSON-RPC Account (or Address)](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#json-rpc-accounts)
 or [Local Account (Private Key, etc)](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#local-accounts-private-key-mnemonic-etc)
. If set to `null`, it is assumed that the transport will handle the filling the sender of the transaction.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      account: '0xf39fd6e51aad88f6f4ce6ab8827279cfffb92266'
    })

### accessList (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#accesslist-optional)

*   **Type:** `[AccessList](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#accesslist) `

The access list.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      accessList: [{ \
        address: '0xf39fd6e51aad88f6f4ce6ab8827279cfffb92266',\
        storageKeys: ['0x1'],\
      }],
    })

### authorizationList (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#authorizationlist-optional)

*   **Type:** `AuthorizationList`

Signed EIP-7702 Authorization list.

    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({ 
      contractAddress: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2', 
    }) 
     
    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: account.address,
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      authorizationList: [authorization], 
    })

### args (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#args-optional)

*   **Type:** Inferred from ABI.

Arguments to pass to function call.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420] 
    })

### chain (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#chain-optional)

*   **Type:** `[Chain](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#chain) `
*   **Default:** `walletClient.chain`

The target chain. If there is a mismatch between the wallet's current chain & the target chain, an error will be thrown.

The chain is also used to infer its request type (e.g. the Celo chain has a `gatewayFee` that you can pass through to `sendTransaction`).

    import { optimism } from 'viem/chains'
     
    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      chain: optimism, 
    })

### dataSuffix[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#datasuffix)

*   **Type:** `Hex`

Data to append to the end of the calldata. Useful for adding a ["domain" tag](https://opensea.notion.site/opensea/Seaport-Order-Attributions-ec2d69bf455041a5baa490941aad307f)
.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      dataSuffix: '0xdeadbeef'
    })

### gas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#gas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

The gas limit for the transaction. Note that passing a gas limit also skips the gas estimation step.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      gas: 69420n, 
    })

### gasPrice (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#gasprice-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

The price (in wei) to pay per gas. Only applies to [Legacy Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#legacy-transaction)
.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      gasPrice: parseGwei('20'), 
    })

### maxFeePerGas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#maxfeepergas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Total fee per gas (in wei), inclusive of `maxPriorityFeePerGas`. Only applies to [EIP-1559 Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#eip-1559-transaction)

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      maxFeePerGas: parseGwei('20'),  
    })

### maxPriorityFeePerGas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#maxpriorityfeepergas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Max priority fee per gas (in wei). Only applies to [EIP-1559 Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#eip-1559-transaction)

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      maxFeePerGas: parseGwei('20'),
      maxPriorityFeePerGas: parseGwei('2'), 
    })

### nonce (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#nonce-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`

Unique number identifying this transaction.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      nonce: 69
    })

### value (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#value-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`

Value in wei sent with this transaction.

    await walletClient.writeContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      value: parseEther('1') 
    })

Live Example[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContract#live-example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

Check out the usage of `writeContract` in the live [Writing to Contracts Example](https://stackblitz.com/github/wevm/viem/tree/main/examples/contracts_writing-to-contracts)
 below.

[Suggest changes to this page](https://github.com/wevm/viem/edit/main/site/pages/docs/contract/writeContract.md)

# writeContractSync · Viem

[Skip to content](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#vocs-content)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

Search...

⌘

K

writeContractSync
=================

Executes a write function on a contract, and waits for the transaction to be included in a block. Returns the transaction receipt.

A "write" function on a Solidity contract modifies the state of the blockchain. These types of functions require gas to be executed, and hence a [Transaction](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms)
 is needed to be broadcast in order to change the state.

Internally, `writeContractSync` uses a [Wallet Client](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet)
 to call the [`sendTransactionSync` action](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync)
 with [ABI-encoded `data`](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/encodeFunctionData)
.

Usage[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#usage)

---------------------------------------------------------------

Below is a very basic example of how to execute a write function on a contract (with no arguments).

While you can use `writeContractSync` [by itself](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#standalone)
, it is highly recommended to pair it with `[simulateContract](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/simulateContract) ` to validate that the contract write will execute without errors.

example.tsabi.tsconfig.ts

    import { account, publicClient, walletClient } from './config'
    import { wagmiAbi } from './abi'
     
    const { request } = await publicClient.simulateContract({
      account,
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
    })
    const receipt = await walletClient.writeContractSync(request)

### Passing Arguments[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#passing-arguments)

If your function requires argument(s), you can pass them through with the `args` attribute.

TypeScript types for `args` will be inferred from the function name & ABI, to guard you from inserting the wrong values.

For example, the `mint` function name below requires a **tokenId** argument, and it is typed as `[number]`.

example.tsabi.tsconfig.ts

    import { account, walletClient } from './client'
    import { wagmiAbi } from './abi'
     
    const { request } = await publicClient.simulateContract({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      account
    })
    const receipt = await walletClient.writeContractSync(request)

### Standalone[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#standalone)

If you don't need to perform validation on the contract write, you can also use it by itself:

example.tsabi.tsconfig.ts

    import { account, walletClient } from './config'
    import { wagmiAbi } from './abi'
     
    const receipt = await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      account,
    })

Return Value[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#return-value)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[TransactionReceipt](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#transaction-receipt) `

A [Transaction receipt](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#transaction-receipt)
.

Parameters[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

### address[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#address)

*   **Type:** `[Address](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#address) `

The contract address.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2', 
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420]
    })

### abi[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#abi)

*   **Type:** `[Abi](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#abi) `

The contract's ABI.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi, 
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420]
    })

### functionName[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#functionname)

*   **Type:** `string`

A function to extract from the ABI.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint', 
      args: [69420]
    })

### account[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#account)

*   **Type:** `Account | Address | null`

The Account to write to the contract from.

Accepts a [JSON-RPC Account (or Address)](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#json-rpc-accounts)
 or [Local Account (Private Key, etc)](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#local-accounts-private-key-mnemonic-etc)
. If set to `null`, it is assumed that the transport will handle the filling the sender of the transaction.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      account: '0xf39fd6e51aad88f6f4ce6ab8827279cfffb92266'
    })

### accessList (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#accesslist-optional)

*   **Type:** `[AccessList](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#accesslist) `

The access list.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      accessList: [{ \
        address: '0xf39fd6e51aad88f6f4ce6ab8827279cfffb92266',\
        storageKeys: ['0x1'],\
      }],
    })

### authorizationList (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#authorizationlist-optional)

*   **Type:** `AuthorizationList`

Signed EIP-7702 Authorization list.

    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({ 
      contractAddress: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2', 
    }) 
     
    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: account.address,
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      authorizationList: [authorization], 
    })

### args (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#args-optional)

*   **Type:** Inferred from ABI.

Arguments to pass to function call.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420] 
    })

### chain (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#chain-optional)

*   **Type:** `[Chain](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#chain) `
*   **Default:** `walletClient.chain`

The target chain. If there is a mismatch between the wallet's current chain & the target chain, an error will be thrown.

The chain is also used to infer its request type (e.g. the Celo chain has a `gatewayFee` that you can pass through to `sendTransactionSync`).

    import { optimism } from 'viem/chains'
     
    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      chain: optimism, 
    })

### dataSuffix[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#datasuffix)

*   **Type:** `Hex`

Data to append to the end of the calldata. Useful for adding a ["domain" tag](https://opensea.notion.site/opensea/Seaport-Order-Attributions-ec2d69bf455041a5baa490941aad307f)
.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      dataSuffix: '0xdeadbeef'
    })

### gas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#gas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

The gas limit for the transaction. Note that passing a gas limit also skips the gas estimation step.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      gas: 69420n, 
    })

### gasPrice (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#gasprice-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

The price (in wei) to pay per gas. Only applies to [Legacy Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#legacy-transaction)
.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      gasPrice: parseGwei('20'), 
    })

### maxFeePerGas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#maxfeepergas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Total fee per gas (in wei), inclusive of `maxPriorityFeePerGas`. Only applies to [EIP-1559 Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#eip-1559-transaction)

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      maxFeePerGas: parseGwei('20'),  
    })

### maxPriorityFeePerGas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#maxpriorityfeepergas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Max priority fee per gas (in wei). Only applies to [EIP-1559 Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#eip-1559-transaction)

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      maxFeePerGas: parseGwei('20'),
      maxPriorityFeePerGas: parseGwei('2'), 
    })

### nonce (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#nonce-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`

Unique number identifying this transaction.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      nonce: 69
    })

### pollingInterval (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#pollinginterval-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`
*   **Default:** `walletClient.pollingInterval`

The polling interval to poll for the transaction receipt.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      pollingInterval: 1_000
    })

### throwOnReceiptRevert (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#throwonreceiptrevert-optional)

*   **Type:** `boolean`

Whether to throw an error if the transaction was detected as reverted.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      throwOnReceiptRevert: true
    })

### timeout (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#timeout-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`
*   **Default:** `chain.blockTime * 3`

The timeout to wait for the transaction receipt.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      timeout: 20_000
    })

### value (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/contract/writeContractSync#value-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`

Value in wei sent with this transaction.

    await walletClient.writeContractSync({
      address: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2',
      abi: wagmiAbi,
      functionName: 'mint',
      args: [69420],
      value: parseEther('1') 
    })

[Suggest changes to this page](https://github.com/wevm/viem/edit/main/site/pages/docs/contract/writeContractSync.md)

# sendTransactionSync · Viem

[Skip to content](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#vocs-content)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

Search...

⌘

K

sendTransactionSync
===================

Creates, signs, and sends a new transaction to the network, and waits for the transaction to be included in a block. Returns the transaction receipt.

Usage[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#usage)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

example.tsconfig.ts

    import { account, walletClient } from './config'
     
    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({ 
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

### Account Hoisting[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#account-hoisting)

If you do not wish to pass an `account` to every `sendTransaction`, you can also hoist the Account on the Wallet Client (see `config.ts`).

[Learn more](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#account)
.

example.tsconfig.ts (JSON-RPC Account)config.ts (Local Account)

    import { walletClient } from './config'
     
    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({ 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

Returns[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[TransactionReceipt](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#transaction-receipt) `

The [Transaction receipt](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#transaction-receipt)
.

Parameters[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### account[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#account)

*   **Type:** `Account | Address | null`

The Account to send the transaction from.

Accepts a [JSON-RPC Account](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#json-rpc-accounts)
 or [Local Account (Private Key, etc)](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#local-accounts-private-key-mnemonic-etc)
. If set to `null`, it is assumed that the transport will handle filling the sender of the transaction.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account: '0xf39fd6e51aad88f6f4ce6ab8827279cfffb92266', 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

### to[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#to)

*   **Type:** `0x${string}`

The transaction recipient or contract address.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8', 
      value: 1000000000000000000n,
      nonce: 69
    })

### accessList (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#accesslist-optional)

*   **Type:** `[AccessList](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#accesslist) `

The access list.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      accessList: [ \
        {\
          address: '0x1',\
          storageKeys: ['0x1'],\
        },\
      ],
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
    })

### authorizationList (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#authorizationlist-optional)

*   **Type:** `AuthorizationList`

Signed EIP-7702 Authorization list.

    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({ 
      account,
      contractAddress: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2', 
    }) 
     
    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      authorizationList: [authorization], 
      data: '0xdeadbeef',
      to: account.address,
    })

### blobs (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#blobs-optional)

*   **Type:** `Hex[]`

Blobs for [Blob Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/guides/blob-transactions)
.

    import * as cKzg from 'c-kzg'
    import { toBlobs, setupKzg, stringToHex } from 'viem'
    import { mainnetTrustedSetupPath } from 'viem/node'
     
    const kzg = setupKzg(cKzg, mainnetTrustedSetupPath) 
     
    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      blobs: toBlobs({ data: stringToHex('blobby blob!') }), 
      kzg,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8'
    })

### chain (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#chain-optional)

*   **Type:** `[Chain](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#chain) `
*   **Default:** `walletClient.chain`

The target chain. If there is a mismatch between the wallet's current chain & the target chain, an error will be thrown.

The chain is also used to infer its request type (e.g. the Celo chain has a `gatewayFee` that you can pass through to `sendTransactionSync`).

    import { optimism } from 'viem/chains'
     
    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      chain: optimism, 
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

### data (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#data-optional)

*   **Type:** `0x${string}`

A contract hashed method call with encoded args.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      data: '0xc02aaa39b223fe8d0a0e5c4f27ead9083c756cc2', 
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

### gas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#gas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

The gas limit of the transaction. If missing, it will be estimated.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      gas: 21000n, 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1') 
    })

### gasPrice (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#gasprice-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

The price (in wei) to pay per gas. Only applies to [Legacy Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#legacy-transaction)
.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      gasPrice: parseGwei('20'), 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1') 
    })

### kzg (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#kzg-optional)

*   **Type:** `KZG`

KZG implementation for [Blob Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/guides/blob-transactions)
.

See `[setupKzg](https://viem.sh/docs/utilities/setupKzg) ` for more information.

    import * as cKzg from 'c-kzg'
    import { toBlobs, setupKzg, stringToHex } from 'viem'
    import { mainnetTrustedSetupPath } from 'viem/node'
     
    const kzg = setupKzg(cKzg, mainnetTrustedSetupPath) 
     
    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      blobs: toBlobs({ data: stringToHex('blobby blob!') }), 
      kzg, 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8'
    })

### maxFeePerGas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#maxfeepergas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Total fee per gas (in wei), inclusive of `maxPriorityFeePerGas`. Only applies to [EIP-1559 Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#eip-1559-transaction)

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      maxFeePerGas: parseGwei('20'),  
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1')
    })

### maxPriorityFeePerGas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#maxpriorityfeepergas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Max priority fee per gas (in wei). Only applies to [EIP-1559 Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#eip-1559-transaction)

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      maxFeePerGas: parseGwei('20'),
      maxPriorityFeePerGas: parseGwei('2'), 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1')
    })

### nonce (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#nonce-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`

Unique number identifying this transaction.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n,
      nonce: 69
    })

### pollingInterval (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#pollinginterval-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`
*   **Default:** `walletClient.pollingInterval`

The polling interval to poll for the transaction receipt.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n,
      nonce: 69,
      pollingInterval: 1_000
    })

### throwOnReceiptRevert (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#throwonreceiptrevert-optional)

*   **Type:** `boolean`

Whether to throw an error if the transaction was detected as reverted.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n,
      nonce: 69,
      throwOnReceiptRevert: true
    })

### timeout (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#timeout-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`
*   **Default:** `chain.blockTime * 3`

The timeout to wait for the transaction receipt.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n,
      nonce: 69,
      timeout: 20_000
    })

### value (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#value-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Value in wei sent with this transaction.

    const receipt = await walletClient.sendTransactionSync({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1'), 
      nonce: 69
    })

Tips[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#tips)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

*   For dapps: When using this action, it is assumed that the user has connected to their wallet (e.g. given permission for the dapp to access their accounts via `[requestAddresses](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/requestAddresses) `). You can also check if the user has granted access to their accounts via `[getAddresses](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/getAddresses) `

JSON-RPC Methods[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync#json-rpc-methods)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   JSON-RPC Accounts:
    *   `[eth_sendTransaction](https://ethereum.org/en/developers/docs/apis/json-rpc/#eth_sendtransaction) `
*   Local Accounts:
    *   `eth_sendRawTransactionSync`

[Suggest changes to this page](https://github.com/wevm/viem/edit/main/site/pages/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransactionSync.md)

Copy page for AI

⌘

# signTransaction · Viem

[Skip to content](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#vocs-content)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

Search...

⌘

K

signTransaction
===============

Signs a transaction.

Usage[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#usage)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

example.tsconfig.ts

    import { account, walletClient } from './config'
     
    const request = await walletClient.prepareTransactionRequest({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })
     
    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction(request) 
    // 0x02f850018203118080825208808080c080a04012522854168b27e5dc3d5839bab5e6b39e1a0ffd343901ce1622e3d64b48f1a04e00902ae0502c4728cbf12156290df99c3ed7de85b1dbfe20b5c36931733a33
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendRawTransaction(signature)

### Account Hoisting[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#account-hoisting)

If you do not wish to pass an `account` to every `prepareTransactionRequest`, you can also hoist the Account on the Wallet Client (see `config.ts`).

[Learn more](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#account)
.

example.tsconfig.ts (JSON-RPC Account)config.ts (Local Account)

    import { walletClient } from './config'
     
    const request = await walletClient.prepareTransactionRequest({
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })
     
    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction(request) 
    // 0x02f850018203118080825208808080c080a04012522854168b27e5dc3d5839bab5e6b39e1a0ffd343901ce1622e3d64b48f1a04e00902ae0502c4728cbf12156290df99c3ed7de85b1dbfe20b5c36931733a33
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendRawTransaction(signature)

Returns[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`[Hex](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#hex) `

The signed serialized transaction.

Parameters[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

### account[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#account)

*   **Type:** `Account | Address`

The Account to send the transaction from.

Accepts a [JSON-RPC Account](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#json-rpc-accounts)
 or [Local Account (Private Key, etc)](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#local-accounts-private-key-mnemonic-etc)
.

    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      account: '0xf39fd6e51aad88f6f4ce6ab8827279cfffb92266', 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

### to[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#to)

*   **Type:** `0x${string}`

The transaction recipient or contract address.

    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8', 
      value: 1000000000000000000n,
      nonce: 69
    })

### accessList (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#accesslist-optional)

*   **Type:** `[AccessList](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#accesslist) `

The access list.

    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      accessList: [ \
        {\
          address: '0x1',\
          storageKeys: ['0x1'],\
        },\
      ],
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
    })

### authorizationList (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#authorizationlist-optional)

*   **Type:** `AuthorizationList`

Signed EIP-7702 Authorization list.

    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({ 
      account,
      contractAddress: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2', 
    }) 
     
    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      account,
      authorizationList: [authorization], 
      data: '0xdeadbeef',
      to: account.address,
    })

### blobs (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#blobs-optional)

*   **Type:** `Hex[]`

Blobs for [Blob Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/guides/blob-transactions)
.

    import * as cKzg from 'c-kzg'
    import { toBlobs, setupKzg, stringToHex } from 'viem'
    import { mainnetTrustedSetupPath } from 'viem/node'
     
    const kzg = setupKzg(cKzg, mainnetTrustedSetupPath) 
     
    const hash = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      account,
      blobs: toBlobs({ data: stringToHex('blobby blob!') }), 
      kzg,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8'
    })

### chain (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#chain-optional)

*   **Type:** `[Chain](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#chain) `
*   **Default:** `walletClient.chain`

The target chain. If there is a mismatch between the wallet's current chain & the target chain, an error will be thrown.

The chain is also used to infer its request type (e.g. the Celo chain has a `gatewayFee` that you can pass through to `signTransaction`).

    import { optimism } from 'viem/chains'
     
    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      chain: optimism, 
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

### data (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#data-optional)

*   **Type:** `0x${string}`

A contract hashed method call with encoded args.

    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      data: '0xc02aaa39b223fe8d0a0e5c4f27ead9083c756cc2', 
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

### gas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#gas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

The gas limit of the transaction. If missing, it will be estimated.

    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      account,
      gas: 21000n, 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1') 
    })

### gasPrice (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#gasprice-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

The price (in wei) to pay per gas. Only applies to [Legacy Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#legacy-transaction)
.

    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      account,
      gasPrice: parseGwei('20'), 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1') 
    })

### kzg (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#kzg-optional)

*   **Type:** `KZG`

KZG implementation for [Blob Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/guides/blob-transactions)
.

See `[setupKzg](https://viem.sh/docs/utilities/setupKzg) ` for more information.

    import { toBlobs, setupKzg, stringToHex } from 'viem'
    import { mainnetTrustedSetupPath } from 'viem/node'

      account,
      blobs: toBlobs({ data: stringToHex('blobby blob!') }), 
      kzg, 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8'
    })

### maxFeePerGas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#maxfeepergas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Total fee per gas (in wei), inclusive of `maxPriorityFeePerGas`. Only applies to [EIP-1559 Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#eip-1559-transaction)

    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      account,
      maxFeePerGas: parseGwei('20'),  
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1')
    })

### maxPriorityFeePerGas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#maxpriorityfeepergas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Max priority fee per gas (in wei). Only applies to [EIP-1559 Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#eip-1559-transaction)

      account,
      maxFeePerGas: parseGwei('20'),
      maxPriorityFeePerGas: parseGwei('2'), 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1')
    })

### nonce (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#nonce-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`

Unique number identifying this transaction.

    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n,
      nonce: 69
    })

### value (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction#value-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Value in wei sent with this transaction.

    const signature = await walletClient.signTransaction({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1'), 
      nonce: 69
    })

[Suggest changes to this page](https://github.com/wevm/viem/edit/main/site/pages/docs/actions/wallet/signTransaction.md)

Copy page for AI

# sendTransaction · Viem

[Skip to content](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#vocs-content)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

Search...

⌘

K

sendTransaction
===============

Creates, signs, and sends a new transaction to the network.

Usage[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#usage)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

example.tsconfig.ts

    import { account, walletClient } from './config'
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({ 
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })
    // '0x...'

### Account Hoisting[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#account-hoisting)

If you do not wish to pass an `account` to every `sendTransaction`, you can also hoist the Account on the Wallet Client (see `config.ts`).

[Learn more](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#account)
.

example.tsconfig.ts (JSON-RPC Account)config.ts (Local Account)

    import { walletClient } from './config'
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({ 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })
    // '0x...'

Returns[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`[Hash](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#hash) `

The [Transaction](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#transaction)
 hash.

Parameters[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

### account[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#account)

*   **Type:** `Account | Address | null`

The Account to send the transaction from.

Accepts a [JSON-RPC Account](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#json-rpc-accounts)
 or [Local Account (Private Key, etc)](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#local-accounts-private-key-mnemonic-etc)
. If set to `null`, it is assumed that the transport will handle filling the sender of the transaction.

    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account: '0xf39fd6e51aad88f6f4ce6ab8827279cfffb92266', 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

### to[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#to)

*   **Type:** `0x${string}`

The transaction recipient or contract address.

    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8', 
      value: 1000000000000000000n,
      nonce: 69
    })

### accessList (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#accesslist-optional)

*   **Type:** `[AccessList](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#accesslist) `

The access list.

    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      accessList: [ \
        {\
          address: '0x1',\
          storageKeys: ['0x1'],\
        },\
      ],
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
    })

### authorizationList (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#authorizationlist-optional)

*   **Type:** `AuthorizationList`

Signed EIP-7702 Authorization list.

    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({ 
      account,
      contractAddress: '0xFBA3912Ca04dd458c843e2EE08967fC04f3579c2', 
    }) 
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account,
      authorizationList: [authorization], 
      data: '0xdeadbeef',
      to: account.address,
    })

### blobs (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#blobs-optional)

*   **Type:** `Hex[]`

Blobs for [Blob Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/guides/blob-transactions)
.

    import * as cKzg from 'c-kzg'
    import { toBlobs, setupKzg, stringToHex } from 'viem'
    import { mainnetTrustedSetupPath } from 'viem/node'
     
    const kzg = setupKzg(cKzg, mainnetTrustedSetupPath) 
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account,
      blobs: toBlobs({ data: stringToHex('blobby blob!') }), 
      kzg,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8'
    })

### chain (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#chain-optional)

*   **Type:** `[Chain](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/types#chain) `
*   **Default:** `walletClient.chain`

The target chain. If there is a mismatch between the wallet's current chain & the target chain, an error will be thrown.

The chain is also used to infer its request type (e.g. the Celo chain has a `gatewayFee` that you can pass through to `sendTransaction`).

    import { optimism } from 'viem/chains'
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      chain: optimism, 
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

### data (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#data-optional)

*   **Type:** `0x${string}`

A contract hashed method call with encoded args.

    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      data: '0xc02aaa39b223fe8d0a0e5c4f27ead9083c756cc2', 
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n
    })

### gas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#gas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

The gas limit of the transaction. If missing, it will be estimated.

    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account,
      gas: 21000n, 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1') 
    })

### gasPrice (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#gasprice-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

The price (in wei) to pay per gas. Only applies to [Legacy Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#legacy-transaction)
.

    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account,
      gasPrice: parseGwei('20'), 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1') 
    })

### kzg (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#kzg-optional)

*   **Type:** `KZG`

KZG implementation for [Blob Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/guides/blob-transactions)
.

See `[setupKzg](https://viem.sh/docs/utilities/setupKzg) ` for more information.

    import * as cKzg from 'c-kzg'
    import { toBlobs, setupKzg, stringToHex } from 'viem'
    import { mainnetTrustedSetupPath } from 'viem/node'
     
    const kzg = setupKzg(cKzg, mainnetTrustedSetupPath) 
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account,
      blobs: toBlobs({ data: stringToHex('blobby blob!') }), 
      kzg, 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8'
    })

### maxFeePerGas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#maxfeepergas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Total fee per gas (in wei), inclusive of `maxPriorityFeePerGas`. Only applies to [EIP-1559 Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#eip-1559-transaction)

    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account,
      maxFeePerGas: parseGwei('20'),  
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1')
    })

### maxPriorityFeePerGas (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#maxpriorityfeepergas-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Max priority fee per gas (in wei). Only applies to [EIP-1559 Transactions](https://viem.sh/docs/glossary/terms#eip-1559-transaction)

    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account,
      maxFeePerGas: parseGwei('20'),
      maxPriorityFeePerGas: parseGwei('2'), 
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1')
    })

### nonce (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#nonce-optional)

*   **Type:** `number`

Unique number identifying this transaction.

    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: 1000000000000000000n,
      nonce: 69
    })

### value (optional)[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#value-optional)

*   **Type:** `bigint`

Value in wei sent with this transaction.

    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      account,
      to: '0x70997970c51812dc3a010c7d01b50e0d17dc79c8',
      value: parseEther('1'), 
      nonce: 69
    })

Tips[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#tips)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

*   For dapps: When using this action, it is assumed that the user has connected to their wallet (e.g. given permission for the dapp to access their accounts via `[requestAddresses](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/requestAddresses) `). You can also check if the user has granted access to their accounts via `[getAddresses](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/getAddresses) `

Live Example[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#live-example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Check out the usage of `sendTransaction` in the live [Sending Transactions Example](https://stackblitz.com/github/wevm/viem/tree/main/examples/transactions_sending-transactions)
 below.

JSON-RPC Methods[](https://viem.sh/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction#json-rpc-methods)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   JSON-RPC Accounts:
    *   `[eth_sendTransaction](https://ethereum.org/en/developers/docs/apis/json-rpc/#eth_sendtransaction) `
*   Local Accounts:
    *   `[eth_sendRawTransaction](https://ethereum.org/en/developers/docs/apis/json-rpc/#eth_sendrawtransaction) `

[Suggest changes to this page](https://github.com/wevm/viem/edit/main/site/pages/docs/actions/wallet/sendTransaction.md)

# Contract Writes with EIP-7702 · Viem

[Skip to content](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/contract-writes#vocs-content)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

Search...

⌘

K

Contract Writes with EIP-7702
=============================

The guide below demonstrates how to perform Contract Writes with EIP-7702 to invoke Contract functions on an Externally Owned Account (EOA).

Overview[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/contract-writes#overview)

------------------------------------------------------------------

Here is an end-to-end overview of how to perform a Contract Write to send a batch of Calls. We will break it down into [Steps](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/contract-writes#steps)
 below.

example.tsconfig.tscontract.tsDelegation.sol

    import { privateKeyToAccount } from 'viem/accounts'
    import { walletClient } from './config'
    import { abi, contractAddress } from './contract'
     
    const eoa = privateKeyToAccount('0x...')
     
    // 1. Authorize designation of the Contract onto the EOA.
    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({
      account: eoa,
      contractAddress,
    })
     
    // 2. Designate the Contract on the EOA, and invoke the 
    //    `initialize` function.
    const hash = await walletClient.writeContract({
      abi,
      address: eoa.address,
      authorizationList: [authorization],
      //                  ↑ 3. Pass the Authorization as a parameter.
      functionName: 'initialize',
    })

Steps[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/contract-writes#steps)

------------------------------------------------------------

### 1\. Set up Smart Contract[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/contract-writes#1-set-up-smart-contract)

We will need to set up a Smart Contract to designate on the Account. For the purposes of this guide, we will [create](https://book.getfoundry.sh/reference/forge/forge-init)
 and [deploy](https://book.getfoundry.sh/forge/deploying)
 a simple demonstration `Delegation.sol` contract, however, you can use any existing deployed contract.

Firstly, [deploy a Contract](https://book.getfoundry.sh/forge/deploying)
 to the Network with the following source:

Delegation.sol

    pragma solidity ^0.8.20;
     
    contract Delegation {
      event Log(string message);
     
      function initialize() external payable {
        emit Log('Hello, world!');
      }
     
      function ping() external pure {
        emit Log('Pong!');
      }
    }

### 2\. Set up Client & Account[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/contract-writes#2-set-up-client--account)

Next, we will need to set up a Client and a "Relay Account" that will be responsible for executing the EIP-7702 Contract Write.

config.ts

    import { createWalletClient, http } from 'viem'
    import { sepolia } from 'viem/chains'
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from 'viem/accounts'
     
    export const relay = privateKeyToAccount('0x...')
     
    export const walletClient = createWalletClient({
      account: relay,
      chain: sepolia,
      transport: http(),
    })

### 3\. Authorize Contract Designation[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/contract-writes#3-authorize-contract-designation)

We will need to sign an Authorization to designate the Contract to the Account.

In the example below, we are instantiating an existing EOA (`account`) and using it to sign the Authorization – this will be the Account that will be used for delegation.

example.tscontract.tsconfig.ts

    import { walletClient } from './config'
    import { contractAddress } from './contract'
     
    const eoa = privateKeyToAccount('0x...') 
     
    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({ 
      account: eoa, 
      contractAddress, 
    }) 

### 4\. Execute Contract Write[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/contract-writes#4-execute-contract-write)

We can now designate the Contract on the Account (and execute the `initialize` function) by sending an EIP-7702 Contract Write.

example.tscontract.tsconfig.ts

    import { walletClient } from './config'
    import { abi, contractAddress } from './contract'
     
    const eoa = privateKeyToAccount('0x...')
     
    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({
      account: eoa,
      contractAddress,
    })
     
    const hash = await walletClient.writeContract({ 
      abi, 
      address: eoa.address, 
      authorizationList: [authorization], 
      functionName: 'initialize', 
    }) 

### 5\. (Optional) Interact with the Delegated Account[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/contract-writes#5-optional-interact-with-the-delegated-account)

Now that we have designated a Contract onto the Account, we can interact with it by invoking its functions.

Note that we no longer need to use an Authorization!

example.tscontract.tsconfig.ts

    import { walletClient } from './config'
    import { abi } from './contract'
     
    const eoa = privateKeyToAccount('0x...')
     
    const hash = await walletClient.writeContract({
      abi,
      address: eoa.address,
      functionName: 'ping', 
    })

### Note: Self-executing EIP-7702[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/contract-writes#note-self-executing-eip-7702)

If the signer of the Authorization (ie. the EOA) is also executing the Transaction, you will need to pass `executor: 'self'` to `signAuthorization`.

This is because `authorization.nonce` must be incremented by 1 over `transaction.nonce`, so we will need to hint to `signAuthorization` that this is the case.

example.tsconfig.tscontract.ts

    import { walletClient } from './config'
    import { abi, contractAddress } from './contract'
     
    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({
      account: eoa, 
      contractAddress,
      executor: 'self', 
    })
     
    const hash = await walletClient.writeContract({
      abi,
      address: eoa.address, 
      address: walletClient.account.address, 
      authorizationList: [authorization],
      functionName: 'initialize',
    })

[Suggest changes to this page](https://github.com/wevm/viem/edit/main/site/pages/docs/eip7702/contract-writes.md)

Copy page for AI

Ask AI...

⌘

I

# Sending Transactions with EIP-7702 · Viem

[Skip to content](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions#vocs-content)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

[![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-light.png)![Logo](https://viem.sh/icon-dark.png)](https://viem.sh/)

Search...

⌘

K

Sending Transactions with EIP-7702
==================================

The guide below demonstrates how to send EIP-7702 Transactions to invoke Contract functions on an Externally Owned Account (EOA).

Overview[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions#overview)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

Here is an end-to-end overview of how to execute an EIP-7702 Transaction to emit a simple event on the EOA's designated contract. We will break it down into [Steps](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions#steps)
 below.

example.tsconfig.tscontract.tsDelegation.sol

    import { encodeFunctionData } from 'viem'
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from 'viem/accounts'
    import { walletClient } from './config'
    import { abi, contractAddress } from './contract'
     
    const eoa = privateKeyToAccount('0x...')
     
    // 1. Authorize designation of the Contract onto the EOA.
    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({
      account: eoa,
      contractAddress,
    })
     
    // 2. Designate the Contract on the EOA, and invoke the 
    //    `initialize` function.
    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      authorizationList: [authorization],
      //                  ↑ 3. Pass the Authorization as a parameter.
      data: encodeFunctionData({
        abi,
        functionName: 'initialize',
      }),
      to: eoa.address,
    })

Steps[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions#steps)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

### 1\. Set up Smart Contract[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions#1-set-up-smart-contract)

We will need to set up a Smart Contract to designate on the Account. For the purposes of this guide, we will [create](https://book.getfoundry.sh/reference/forge/forge-init)
 and [deploy](https://book.getfoundry.sh/forge/deploying)
 a simple demonstration `Delegation.sol` contract, however, you can use any existing deployed contract.

Firstly, [deploy a Contract](https://book.getfoundry.sh/forge/deploying)
 to the Network with the following source:

Delegation.sol

    pragma solidity ^0.8.20;
     
    contract Delegation {
      event Log(string message);
     
      function initialize() external payable {
        emit Log('Hello, world!');
      }
     
     
      function ping() external pure {
        emit Log('Pong!');
      }
    }

### 2\. Set up Client & Account[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions#2-set-up-client--account)

Next, we will need to set up a Client and a "Relay Account" that will be responsible for executing the EIP-7702 Transaction.

config.ts

    import { createWalletClient, http } from 'viem'
    import { sepolia } from 'viem/chains'
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from 'viem/accounts'
     
    export const relay = privateKeyToAccount('0x...')
     
    export const walletClient = createWalletClient({
      account: relay,
      chain: sepolia,
      transport: http(),
    })

### 3\. Authorize Contract Designation[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions#3-authorize-contract-designation)

We will need to sign an Authorization to designate the Contract to the Account.

In the example below, we are instantiating an existing EOA (`account`) and using it to sign the Authorization – this will be the Account that will be used for delegation.

example.tscontract.tsconfig.ts

    import { walletClient } from './config'
    import { contractAddress } from './contract'
     
    const eoa = privateKeyToAccount('0x...') 
     
    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({ 
      account: eoa, 
      contractAddress, 
    }) 

### 4\. Execute Transaction[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions#4-execute-transaction)

We can now designate the Contract on the Account (and execute the `initialize` function) by sending an EIP-7702 Transaction.

example.tscontract.tsconfig.ts

    import { encodeFunctionData } from 'viem'
    import { walletClient } from './config'
    import { contractAddress } from './contract'
     
    const eoa = privateKeyToAccount('0x...')
     
    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({
      account: eoa,
      contractAddress,
    })
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({ 
      authorizationList: [authorization], 
      data: encodeFunctionData({ 
        abi, 
        functionName: 'initialize', 
      }), 
      to: eoa.address, 
    }) 

### 5\. (Optional) Interact with the Delegated Account[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions#5-optional-interact-with-the-delegated-account)

Now that we have designated a Contract onto the Account, we can interact with it by invoking its functions.

Note that we no longer need to use an Authorization!

example.tscontract.tsconfig.ts

    import { encodeFunctionData } from 'viem'
    import { walletClient } from './config'
     
    const eoa = privateKeyToAccount('0x...')
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      data: encodeFunctionData({
        abi,
        functionName: 'ping',
      }),
      to: eoa.address,
    })

### Note: Self-executing EIP-7702[](https://viem.sh/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions#note-self-executing-eip-7702)

If the signer of the Authorization (ie. the EOA) is also executing the Transaction, you will need to pass `executor: 'self'` to `signAuthorization`.

This is because `authorization.nonce` must be incremented by 1 over `transaction.nonce`, so we will need to hint to `signAuthorization` that this is the case.

example.tsconfig.tscontract.ts

    import { encodeFunctionData } from 'viem'
    import { walletClient } from './config'
    import { contractAddress } from './contract'
     
    const authorization = await walletClient.signAuthorization({
      account: eoa, 
      contractAddress,
      executor: 'self', 
    })
     
    const hash = await walletClient.sendTransaction({
      authorizationList: [authorization],
      data: encodeFunctionData({
        abi,
        functionName: 'initialize',
      }),
      to: eoa.address, 
      to: walletClient.account.address, 
    })

[Suggest changes to this page](https://github.com/wevm/viem/edit/main/site/pages/docs/eip7702/sending-transactions.md)
